\"text\": \"In Kubernetes v1.32, the CNI (Container Network Interface) integration is implemented across several layers. Since the dockershim was removed in v1.24, the kubelet no longer invokes CNI plugins directly; instead it delegates network setup to the container runtime (containerd, CRI-O) via the Container Runtime Interface (CRI). Here is a breakdown of the relevant source files:\\n\\n**CNI Plugin Invocation (via CRI):**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go`: The `createPodSandbox()` function is the core CNI invocation path. It calls `m.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox()` which triggers the container runtime to invoke the CNI plugin chain. `generatePodSandboxConfig()` and `generatePodSandboxLinuxConfig()` prepare the pod sandbox configuration including port mappings and namespace options that the container runtime uses when calling CNI.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`: Implements the CRI client. `RunPodSandbox()` sends the gRPC request to the container runtime which then invokes CNI plugins. `UpdateRuntimeConfig()` propagates the pod CIDR to the runtime's network plugin (comment: 'This translates to an Event notification to the network plugin').\\n\\n**Network Namespace Setup:**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go`: `NetworkNamespaceForPod()` determines whether a pod gets its own network namespace (POD mode) or shares the host network namespace (NODE mode). `NamespacesForPod()` constructs the full NamespaceOption including network namespace settings. `PodSandboxChanged()` detects if the network namespace mode changed, triggering sandbox recreation with new CNI setup.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox_linux.go`: Linux-specific sandbox resource configuration.\\n\\n**IPAM (IP Address Management):**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go`: `updatePodCIDR()` propagates the pod CIDR to the container runtime. The comment on line 54 explicitly states the path: 'kubelet -> generic runtime -> runtime shim -> network plugin'. This CIDR is used by the CNI IPAM plugin.\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go`: `UpdatePodCIDR()` calls `m.runtimeService.UpdateRuntimeConfig()` with the pod CIDR in a `NetworkConfig`, passing it down to the container runtime's network plugin for IPAM.\\n- `pkg/controller/nodeipam/node_ipam_controller.go`: Node IPAM controller that assigns pod CIDRs (podCIDRs) to Nodes - this is the cluster-level IPAM that assigns IP ranges per node.\\n- `pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidr_allocator.go`: Defines the `CIDRAllocator` interface and allocator types (RangeAllocator, CloudAllocator, IPAMFromCluster, IPAMFromCloud).\\n- `pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/range_allocator.go`: Range-based CIDR allocator that allocates pod CIDRs to nodes from the cluster CIDR range.\\n\\n**Network Plugin Manager (coordinates CNI calls):**\\n- `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go`: `kubeGenericRuntimeManager` is the network plugin manager.
